The page explicitly shows DUAL-BATCH PROCESSING — running two loads through... ### CUT

- `P.1`
  Equation:

  \[X_{\mathrm{P_1}}^+ = A_{\mathrm{P_1}} X_{\mathrm{P_1}}^-, \qquad A_{\mathrm{P_1}} = T_{\mathrm{CUT}}^{-1} \Phi_{\mathrm{P_1}}^{\mathrm{AQM}} T_{\mathrm{CUT}}\]

  Variable legend: `X=(kappa,varphi,ell,b)` with containment, phase, liquid flux, and boundary integrity.
  Reading: settle phase / circulation command / fluid conduit line.
  Confidence: strong

- `P.10`
  Equation:

  \[u_{\mathrm{P_1}}^+ = U_{\mathrm{P_1}}u_{\mathrm{P_1}}^-, \qquad U_{\mathrm{P_1}} = T_{\mathrm{wave}}^{-1} \Phi_{\mathrm{P_1}}^{\mathrm{AQM}} T_{\mathrm{wave}}, \qquad \|U_{\mathrm{P_1}}\| \le 1\]

  Variable legend: `u` is the wave profile; `U_line` is the contraction-compatible update.
  Reading: settle phase / circulation command / fluid conduit line.
  Confidence: strong

## Direct Operational Meaning

A hydraulic distillation page: two sequential streams (two "charges") are circulated, clamped, and committed — while the margin labels name the physical routing elements that make the loop replayable. Process statistics: 60 circulation commands (qo-); 18 valve/clamp checkpoints (ckh/kch); 13 infusion-stabilize cycles (shedy); 6 completion markers (daiin).

## Mathematical Extraction

Across the formal lenses, `f78r` behaves as a fixed-point purification page with N_qo=51, N_valve=10, and N_seal=2. The governing update is x_(n+1) = V(C(x_n)); stop when ||x_(n+1)-x_n|| <= eps, then publish y = S(x_*).

## Mythic Extraction

`f78r` is a bathhouse-laboratory chamber: descend through linked pools, purify by circulation, prove stability at the clamps, and only then carry the living fluid onward.
